## Details

The CodeBoarding system operates as a multi-stage pipeline that transforms raw source code into high-level architectural documentation. The process begins with the Orchestration & Workflow Manager initializing the environment and triggering the Incremental Analysis Controller to identify modified code. The Static Analysis Engine then extracts structural metadata, which is enriched by the Agentic Intelligence Core using LLMs. Simultaneously, the Health & Quality Monitor evaluates code metrics. Finally, the Rendering & Output Engine compiles these structural, semantic, and health insights into visual and textual artifacts, all supported by a unified Persistence & Provider Infrastructure layer.

### Orchestration & Workflow Manager [[Expand]](./Orchestration_Workflow_Manager.md)
The central nervous system of the application. It handles CLI interactions, initializes the environment, manages the high-level execution sequence of the analysis pipeline, and coordinates between the repository and the analysis engines.

- `codeboarding_workflows.orchestration.run_analysis_pipeline`:25-48
- `codeboarding_cli.commands.full_analysis`
- `diagram_analysis.diagram_generator.DiagramGenerator`:50-517

### Incremental Analysis Controller [[Expand]](./Incremental_Analysis_Controller.md)
Optimizes performance by performing semantic diffing between repository states. It identifies changed files and affected code clusters to ensure that only modified components are re-analyzed by the LSP and LLM layers.


**Related Classes/Methods**:

- `repo_utils.change_detector.ChangeSet`:224-292
- `diagram_analysis.incremental_pipeline.run_incremental_pipeline`:167-285
- `static_analyzer.cluster_change_analyzer.ClusterChangeAnalyzer`:80-329

### Static Analysis Engine [[Expand]](./Static_Analysis_Engine.md)
A multi-language engine that leverages the Language Server Protocol (LSP) to extract structural data. It builds Call Flow Graphs (CFG), resolves symbol tables, and maps code relationships into a unified internal model.


**Related Classes/Methods**:

- `static_analyzer.engine.lsp_client.LSPClient`:31-813
- `static_analyzer.engine.call_graph_builder.CallGraphBuilder`:23-302
- `static_analyzer.engine.language_adapter.LanguageAdapter`:22-363

### Agentic Intelligence Core
A decentralized layer of LLM-powered agents (Abstraction and Details agents) that interpret static analysis data. It uses specialized prompts to generate architectural summaries, explain complex logic, and provide intelligence that static tools cannot.


**Related Classes/Methods**:

- `agents.abstraction_agent.AbstractionAgent`:38-177
- `agents.details_agent.DetailsAgent`:37-249
- `agents.agent.CodeBoardingAgent`:34-407

### Health & Quality Monitor
Analyzes the structural data produced by the engine to calculate software metrics such as coupling, cohesion, and cyclomatic complexity. It identifies architectural smells like circular dependencies or God classes.


**Related Classes/Methods**:

- `health.runner.run_health_checks`:187-236
- `health.checks.coupling.check_fan_out`:35-85

### Rendering & Output Engine [[Expand]](./Rendering_Output_Engine.md)
The final stage of the pipeline that transforms processed analysis and agent insights into user-consumable formats, including Mermaid.js diagrams, Markdown documentation, and interactive HTML reports.

### Persistence & Provider Infrastructure [[Expand]](./Persistence_Provider_Infrastructure.md)
Provides the foundational services for the system, including LLM provider configuration (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.), DuckDB/SQLite persistence for job tracking, and caching mechanisms to prevent redundant LLM calls.
